3926       ciKlass* ak = ciArrayKlass::make(env()->Object_klass());
3927       const Type* akls = TypeKlassPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, ak, Type::Offset(0));
3928       Node* cast = new CastPPNode(klass_node, akls);
3929       cast->init_req(0, control());
3930       klass_node = _gvn.transform(cast);
3931     }
3932 
3933     Node* original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3934     // ArrayCopyNode:Ideal may transform the ArrayCopyNode to
3935     // loads/stores but it is legal only if we're sure the
3936     // Arrays.copyOf would succeed. So we need all input arguments
3937     // to the copyOf to be validated, including that the copy to the
3938     // new array won't trigger an ArrayStoreException. That subtype
3939     // check can be optimized if we know something on the type of
3940     // the input array from type speculation.
3941     if (_gvn.type(klass_node)->singleton() && !stopped()) {
3942       ciKlass* subk   = _gvn.type(original_kls)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3943       ciKlass* superk = _gvn.type(klass_node)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3944 
3945       int test = C->static_subtype_check(superk, subk);
3946       if (test != Compile::SSC_always_true && test != Compile::SSC_always_false) {
3947         const TypeOopPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->is_oopptr();
3948         if (t_original->speculative_type() != NULL) {
3949           original = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(original, t_original->speculative_type(), true);
3950           original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3951         }
3952       }
3953     }
3954 
3955     if (UseFlatArray) {
3956       // Either both or neither new array klass and original array
3957       // klass must be flattened
3958       const TypeAryPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->isa_aryptr();
3959       Node* is_flat = generate_flatArray_guard(klass_node, NULL);
3960       if (t_original == NULL || !t_original->is_not_flat()) {
3961         generate_flatArray_guard(original_kls, bailout);
3962       }
3963       if (is_flat != NULL) {
3964         RegionNode* r = new RegionNode(2);
3965         record_for_igvn(r);
3966         r->init_req(1, control());
3967         set_control(is_flat);
3968         if (t_original == NULL || !t_original->is_not_flat()) {
3969           generate_flatArray_guard(original_kls, r);
3970         }
3971         bailout->add_req(control());
3972         set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
3973       }
3974     }
3975 
3976     // Bail out if either start or end is negative.
3977     generate_negative_guard(start, bailout, &start);
3978     generate_negative_guard(end,   bailout, &end);
3979 
3980     Node* length = end;
3981     if (_gvn.type(start) != TypeInt::ZERO) {
3982       length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, start));
3983     }
3984 
3985     // Bail out if length is negative.
3986     // Without this the new_array would throw
3987     // NegativeArraySizeException but IllegalArgumentException is what
3988     // should be thrown
3989     generate_negative_guard(length, bailout, &length);
3990 
3991     if (bailout->req() > 1) {
3992       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
3993       set_control(_gvn.transform(bailout));
3994       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
3995                     Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
3996     }
3997 
3998     if (!stopped()) {
3999       // How many elements will we copy from the original?
4000       // The answer is MinI(orig_length - start, length).
4001       Node* orig_tail = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(orig_length, start));
4002       Node* moved = generate_min_max(vmIntrinsics::_min, orig_tail, length);
4003 
4004       // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4005       // We know the copy is disjoint but we might not know if the
4006       // oop stores need checking.
4007       // Extreme case:  Arrays.copyOf((Integer[])x, 10, String[].class).
4008       // This will fail a store-check if x contains any non-nulls.
4009 
4010       bool validated = false;
4011       // Reason_class_check rather than Reason_intrinsic because we
4012       // want to intrinsify even if this traps.
4013       if (!too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check)) {
4014         Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(original, klass_node);
4015 
4016         if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
4017           PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4018           set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
4019           uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check,
4020                         Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
4021           assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
4022         }
4023         validated = true;
4024       }
4025 
4026       if (!stopped()) {
4027         newcopy = new_array(klass_node, length, 0);  // no arguments to push
4028 
4029         ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, original, start, newcopy, intcon(0), moved, true, false,
4030                                                 original_kls, klass_node);
4031         if (!is_copyOfRange) {
4032           ac->set_copyof(validated);
4033         } else {
4034           ac->set_copyofrange(validated);
4035         }
4036         Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4037         if (n == ac) {
4038           ac->connect_outputs(this);
4039         } else {
4040           assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
4041           set_all_memory(n);
4042         }
4043       }
4044     }
4045   } // original reexecute is set back here
4046 
4047   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4048   if (!stopped()) {
4049     set_result(newcopy);
4050   }
4051   return true;
4052 }
4053 
4054 
4055 //----------------------generate_virtual_guard---------------------------
4056 // Helper for hashCode and clone.  Peeks inside the vtable to avoid a call.
4057 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_virtual_guard(Node* obj_klass,
4058                                              RegionNode* slow_region) {
4059   ciMethod* method = callee();
4060   int vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4061   assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4062          "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4063   // Get the Method* out of the appropriate vtable entry.
4064   int entry_offset  = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset()) +
4065                      vtable_index*vtableEntry::size_in_bytes() +
4066                      vtableEntry::method_offset_in_bytes();
4067   Node* entry_addr  = basic_plus_adr(obj_klass, entry_offset);
4068   Node* target_call = make_load(NULL, entry_addr, TypePtr::NOTNULL, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
4069 
4070   // Compare the target method with the expected method (e.g., Object.hashCode).
4071   const TypePtr* native_call_addr = TypeMetadataPtr::make(method);
4072 
4073   Node* native_call = makecon(native_call_addr);
4074   Node* chk_native  = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(target_call, native_call));
4075   Node* test_native = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(chk_native, BoolTest::ne));
4076 
4077   return generate_slow_guard(test_native, slow_region);
4078 }
4079 
4080 //-----------------------generate_method_call----------------------------
4081 // Use generate_method_call to make a slow-call to the real
4082 // method if the fast path fails.  An alternative would be to
4083 // use a stub like OptoRuntime::slow_arraycopy_Java.
4084 // This only works for expanding the current library call,
4085 // not another intrinsic.  (E.g., don't use this for making an
4086 // arraycopy call inside of the copyOf intrinsic.)
4087 CallJavaNode*
4088 LibraryCallKit::generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::ID method_id, bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4089   // When compiling the intrinsic method itself, do not use this technique.
4090   guarantee(callee() != C->method(), "cannot make slow-call to self");
4091 
4092   ciMethod* method = callee();
4093   // ensure the JVMS we have will be correct for this call
4094   guarantee(method_id == method->intrinsic_id(), "must match");
4095 
4096   const TypeFunc* tf = TypeFunc::make(method);
4097   CallJavaNode* slow_call;
4098   if (is_static) {
4099     assert(!is_virtual, "");
4100     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4101                            SharedRuntime::get_resolve_static_call_stub(),
4102                            method, bci());
4103   } else if (is_virtual) {
4104     null_check_receiver();
4105     int vtable_index = Method::invalid_vtable_index;
4106     if (UseInlineCaches) {
4107       // Suppress the vtable call
4108     } else {
4109       // hashCode and clone are not a miranda methods,
4110       // so the vtable index is fixed.
4111       // No need to use the linkResolver to get it.
4112        vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4113        assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4114               "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4115     }
4116     slow_call = new CallDynamicJavaNode(tf,
4117                           SharedRuntime::get_resolve_virtual_call_stub(),
4118                           method, vtable_index, bci());
4119   } else {  // neither virtual nor static:  opt_virtual
4120     null_check_receiver();
4121     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4122                                 SharedRuntime::get_resolve_opt_virtual_call_stub(),
4123                                 method, bci());
4124     slow_call->set_optimized_virtual(true);
4125   }
4126   if (CallGenerator::is_inlined_method_handle_intrinsic(this->method(), bci(), callee())) {
4127     // To be able to issue a direct call (optimized virtual or virtual)
4128     // and skip a call to MH.linkTo*/invokeBasic adapter, additional information
4129     // about the method being invoked should be attached to the call site to
4130     // make resolution logic work (see SharedRuntime::resolve_{virtual,opt_virtual}_call_C).
4131     slow_call->set_override_symbolic_info(true);
4132   }
4133   set_arguments_for_java_call(slow_call);
4134   set_edges_for_java_call(slow_call);
4135   return slow_call;
4136 }
4137 
4138 
4139 /**
4140  * Build special case code for calls to hashCode on an object. This call may
4141  * be virtual (invokevirtual) or bound (invokespecial). For each case we generate
4142  * slightly different code.
4143  */
4144 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_hashcode(bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4145   assert(is_static == callee()->is_static(), "correct intrinsic selection");
4146   assert(!(is_virtual && is_static), "either virtual, special, or static");
4147 
4148   enum { _slow_path = 1, _fast_path, _null_path, PATH_LIMIT };
4149 
4150   RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4151   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInt::INT);
4152   PhiNode*    result_io  = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4153   PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4154   Node* obj = argument(0);
4155 
4156   if (obj->is_InlineType() || gvn().type(obj)->is_inlinetypeptr()) {
4157     return false;
4158   }
4159 
4160   if (!is_static) {
4161     // Check for hashing null object
4162     obj = null_check_receiver();
4163     if (stopped())  return true;        // unconditionally null
4164     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, top());
4165     result_val->init_req(_null_path, top());
4166   } else {
4167     // Do a null check, and return zero if null.
4168     // System.identityHashCode(null) == 0
4169     Node* null_ctl = top();
4170     obj = null_check_oop(obj, &null_ctl);
4171     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, null_ctl);
4172     result_val->init_req(_null_path, _gvn.intcon(0));
4173   }
4174 
4175   // Unconditionally null?  Then return right away.
4176   if (stopped()) {
4177     set_control( result_reg->in(_null_path));
4178     if (!stopped())
4179       set_result(result_val->in(_null_path));
4180     return true;
4181   }
4182 
4183   // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.  The
4184   // paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4185   RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4186   record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4187 
4188   // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We pull out
4189   // the vtable entry corresponding to hashCode() from the target object.
4190   // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the native
4191   // Object hashCode() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4192   // guard for non-virtual calls -- the caller is known to be the native
4193   // Object hashCode().
4194   if (is_virtual) {
4195     // After null check, get the object's klass.
4196     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4197     generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4198   }
4199 
4200   // Get the header out of the object, use LoadMarkNode when available
4201   Node* header_addr = basic_plus_adr(obj, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes());
4202   // The control of the load must be NULL. Otherwise, the load can move before
4203   // the null check after castPP removal.
4204   Node* no_ctrl = NULL;
4205   Node* header = make_load(no_ctrl, header_addr, TypeX_X, TypeX_X->basic_type(), MemNode::unordered);
4206 
4207   // Test the header to see if it is unlocked.
4208   // This also serves as guard against inline types (they have the always_locked_pattern set).
4209   Node *lock_mask      = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::biased_lock_mask_in_place);
4210   Node *lmasked_header = _gvn.transform(new AndXNode(header, lock_mask));
4211   Node *unlocked_val   = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::unlocked_value);
4212   Node *chk_unlocked   = _gvn.transform(new CmpXNode( lmasked_header, unlocked_val));
4213   Node *test_unlocked  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_unlocked, BoolTest::ne));
4214 
4215   generate_slow_guard(test_unlocked, slow_region);
4216 
4217   // Get the hash value and check to see that it has been properly assigned.
4218   // We depend on hash_mask being at most 32 bits and avoid the use of
4219   // hash_mask_in_place because it could be larger than 32 bits in a 64-bit
4220   // vm: see markWord.hpp.
4221   Node *hash_mask      = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_mask);
4222   Node *hash_shift     = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_shift);
4223   Node *hshifted_header= _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(header, hash_shift));
4224   // This hack lets the hash bits live anywhere in the mark object now, as long
4225   // as the shift drops the relevant bits into the low 32 bits.  Note that
4226   // Java spec says that HashCode is an int so there's no point in capturing
4227   // an 'X'-sized hashcode (32 in 32-bit build or 64 in 64-bit build).
4228   hshifted_header      = ConvX2I(hshifted_header);
4229   Node *hash_val       = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(hshifted_header, hash_mask));
4230 
4231   Node *no_hash_val    = _gvn.intcon(markWord::no_hash);
4232   Node *chk_assigned   = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode( hash_val, no_hash_val));
4233   Node *test_assigned  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_assigned, BoolTest::eq));
4234 
4235   generate_slow_guard(test_assigned, slow_region);
4236 
4237   Node* init_mem = reset_memory();
4238   // fill in the rest of the null path:
4239   result_io ->init_req(_null_path, i_o());
4240   result_mem->init_req(_null_path, init_mem);
4241 
4242   result_val->init_req(_fast_path, hash_val);
4243   result_reg->init_req(_fast_path, control());
4244   result_io ->init_req(_fast_path, i_o());
4245   result_mem->init_req(_fast_path, init_mem);
4246 
4247   // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to hashCode().
4248   set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4249   if (!stopped()) {
4250     // No need for PreserveJVMState, because we're using up the present state.
4251     set_all_memory(init_mem);
4252     vmIntrinsics::ID hashCode_id = is_static ? vmIntrinsics::_identityHashCode : vmIntrinsics::_hashCode;
4253     CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(hashCode_id, is_virtual, is_static);
4254     Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call);
4255     // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4256     result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4257     result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4258     result_io  ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4259     result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4260   }
4261 
4262   // Return the combined state.
4263   set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_io)  );
4264   set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4265 
4266   set_result(result_reg, result_val);
4267   return true;
4268 }
4269 
4270 //---------------------------inline_native_getClass----------------------------
4271 // public final native Class<?> java.lang.Object.getClass();
4272 //
4273 // Build special case code for calls to getClass on an object.
4274 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getClass() {
4275   Node* obj = argument(0);
4276   if (obj->is_InlineType()) {
4277     ciKlass* vk = _gvn.type(obj)->inline_klass();
4278     set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(vk->java_mirror())));
4279     return true;
4280   }
4281   obj = null_check_receiver();
4282   if (stopped())  return true;
4283   set_result(load_mirror_from_klass(load_object_klass(obj)));
4284   return true;
4285 }
4286 
4287 //-----------------inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass---------------------
4288 // public static native Class<?> sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass();
4289 //
4290 // In the presence of deep enough inlining, getCallerClass() becomes a no-op.
4291 //
4292 // NOTE: This code must perform the same logic as JVM_GetCallerClass
4293 // in that it must skip particular security frames and checks for
4294 // caller sensitive methods.
4295 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass() {
4296 #ifndef PRODUCT
4297   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4298     tty->print_cr("Attempting to inline sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass");
4299   }
4300 #endif
4301 
4302   if (!jvms()->has_method()) {
4303 #ifndef PRODUCT
4304     if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4305       tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because intrinsic was inlined at top level");
4306     }
4307 #endif
4308     return false;
4309   }
4310 
4311   // Walk back up the JVM state to find the caller at the required
4312   // depth.
4313   JVMState* caller_jvms = jvms();
4314 
4315   // Cf. JVM_GetCallerClass
4316   // NOTE: Start the loop at depth 1 because the current JVM state does
4317   // not include the Reflection.getCallerClass() frame.
4318   for (int n = 1; caller_jvms != NULL; caller_jvms = caller_jvms->caller(), n++) {
4319     ciMethod* m = caller_jvms->method();
4320     switch (n) {
4321     case 0:
4322       fatal("current JVM state does not include the Reflection.getCallerClass frame");
4323       break;
4324     case 1:
4325       // Frame 0 and 1 must be caller sensitive (see JVM_GetCallerClass).
4326       if (!m->caller_sensitive()) {
4327 #ifndef PRODUCT
4328         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4329           tty->print_cr("  Bailing out: CallerSensitive annotation expected at frame %d", n);
4330         }
4331 #endif
4332         return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4333       }
4334       break;
4335     default:
4336       if (!m->is_ignored_by_security_stack_walk()) {
4337         // We have reached the desired frame; return the holder class.
4338         // Acquire method holder as java.lang.Class and push as constant.
4339         ciInstanceKlass* caller_klass = caller_jvms->method()->holder();
4340         ciInstance* caller_mirror = caller_klass->java_mirror();
4341         set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(caller_mirror)));
4342 
4343 #ifndef PRODUCT
4344         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4345           tty->print_cr("  Succeeded: caller = %d) %s.%s, JVMS depth = %d", n, caller_klass->name()->as_utf8(), caller_jvms->method()->name()->as_utf8(), jvms()->depth());
4346           tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4347           for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4348             ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4349             tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4350           }
4351         }
4352 #endif
4353         return true;
4354       }
4355       break;
4356     }
4357   }
4358 
4359 #ifndef PRODUCT
4360   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4361     tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because caller depth exceeded inlining depth = %d", jvms()->depth());
4362     tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4363     for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4364       ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4365       tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4366     }
4367   }
4368 #endif
4369 
4370   return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4371 }
4372 
4373 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_conversions(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
4374   Node* arg = argument(0);
4375   Node* result = NULL;
4376 
4377   switch (id) {
4378   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToRawIntBits:    result = new MoveF2INode(arg);  break;
4379   case vmIntrinsics::_intBitsToFloat:       result = new MoveI2FNode(arg);  break;
4380   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToRawLongBits:  result = new MoveD2LNode(arg);  break;
4381   case vmIntrinsics::_longBitsToDouble:     result = new MoveL2DNode(arg);  break;
4382 
4383   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToLongBits: {
4384     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4385     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4386     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeLong::LONG);
4387 
4388     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpDNode(arg, arg));
4389     // Build the boolean node
4390     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4391 
4392     // Branch either way.
4393     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4394     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4395     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4396     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4397     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4398     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4399 
4400     set_control(iftrue);
4401 
4402     static const jlong nan_bits = CONST64(0x7ff8000000000000);
4403     Node *slow_result = longcon(nan_bits); // return NaN
4404     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4405     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4406 
4407     // Else fall through
4408     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4409     set_control(iffalse);
4410 
4411     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveD2LNode(arg)));
4412     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4413 
4414     // Post merge
4415     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4416     record_for_igvn(r);
4417 
4418     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4419     result = phi;
4420     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_long(), "must be");
4421     break;
4422   }
4423 
4424   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToIntBits: {
4425     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4426     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4427     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeInt::INT);
4428 
4429     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpFNode(arg, arg));
4430     // Build the boolean node
4431     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4432 
4433     // Branch either way.
4434     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4435     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4436     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4437     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4438     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4439     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4440 
4441     set_control(iftrue);
4442 
4443     static const jint nan_bits = 0x7fc00000;
4444     Node *slow_result = makecon(TypeInt::make(nan_bits)); // return NaN
4445     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4446     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4447 
4448     // Else fall through
4449     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4450     set_control(iffalse);
4451 
4452     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveF2INode(arg)));
4453     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4454 
4455     // Post merge
4456     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4457     record_for_igvn(r);
4458 
4459     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4460     result = phi;
4461     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_int(), "must be");
4462     break;
4463   }
4464 
4465   default:
4466     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
4467     break;
4468   }
4469   set_result(_gvn.transform(result));
4470   return true;
4471 }
4472 
4473 //----------------------inline_unsafe_copyMemory-------------------------
4474 // public native void Unsafe.copyMemory0(Object srcBase, long srcOffset, Object destBase, long destOffset, long bytes);
4475 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_copyMemory() {
4476   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
4477   null_check_receiver();  // null-check receiver
4478   if (stopped())  return true;
4479 
4480   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
4481 
4482   Node* src_ptr =         argument(1);   // type: oop
4483   Node* src_off = ConvL2X(argument(2));  // type: long
4484   Node* dst_ptr =         argument(4);   // type: oop
4485   Node* dst_off = ConvL2X(argument(5));  // type: long
4486   Node* size    = ConvL2X(argument(7));  // type: long
4487 
4488   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11,
4489          "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
4490 
4491   Node* src = make_unsafe_address(src_ptr, src_off, ACCESS_READ);
4492   Node* dst = make_unsafe_address(dst_ptr, dst_off, ACCESS_WRITE);
4493 
4494   // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4495   // Do not let writes of the copy source or destination float below the copy.
4496   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4497 
4498   Node* thread = _gvn.transform(new ThreadLocalNode());
4499   Node* doing_unsafe_access_addr = basic_plus_adr(top(), thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::doing_unsafe_access_offset()));
4500   BasicType doing_unsafe_access_bt = T_BYTE;
4501   assert((sizeof(bool) * CHAR_BIT) == 8, "not implemented");
4502 
4503   // update volatile field
4504   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(1), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4505 
4506   // Call it.  Note that the length argument is not scaled.
4507   make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
4508                     OptoRuntime::fast_arraycopy_Type(),
4509                     StubRoutines::unsafe_arraycopy(),
4510                     "unsafe_arraycopy",
4511                     TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM,
4512                     src, dst, size XTOP);
4513 
4514   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(0), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4515 
4516   // Do not let reads of the copy destination float above the copy.
4517   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4518 
4519   return true;
4520 }
4521 
4522 //------------------------clone_coping-----------------------------------
4523 // Helper function for inline_native_clone.
4524 void LibraryCallKit::copy_to_clone(Node* obj, Node* alloc_obj, Node* obj_size, bool is_array) {
4525   assert(obj_size != NULL, "");
4526   Node* raw_obj = alloc_obj->in(1);
4527   assert(alloc_obj->is_CheckCastPP() && raw_obj->is_Proj() && raw_obj->in(0)->is_Allocate(), "");
4528 
4529   AllocateNode* alloc = NULL;
4530   if (ReduceBulkZeroing) {
4531     // We will be completely responsible for initializing this object -
4532     // mark Initialize node as complete.
4533     alloc = AllocateNode::Ideal_allocation(alloc_obj, &_gvn);
4534     // The object was just allocated - there should be no any stores!
4535     guarantee(alloc != NULL && alloc->maybe_set_complete(&_gvn), "");
4536     // Mark as complete_with_arraycopy so that on AllocateNode
4537     // expansion, we know this AllocateNode is initialized by an array
4538     // copy and a StoreStore barrier exists after the array copy.
4539     alloc->initialization()->set_complete_with_arraycopy();
4540   }
4541 
4542   Node* size = _gvn.transform(obj_size);
4543   // Exclude the header but include array length to copy by 8 bytes words.
4544   // Can't use base_offset_in_bytes(bt) since basic type is unknown.
4545   int base_off = BarrierSetC2::arraycopy_payload_base_offset(is_array);
4546   Node* countx = size;
4547   countx = _gvn.transform(new SubXNode(countx, MakeConX(base_off)));
4548   countx = _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(countx, intcon(LogBytesPerLong)));
4549 
4550   access_clone(obj, alloc_obj, countx, is_array);
4551 
4552   // Do not let reads from the cloned object float above the arraycopy.
4553   if (alloc != NULL) {
4554     // Do not let stores that initialize this object be reordered with
4555     // a subsequent store that would make this object accessible by
4556     // other threads.
4557     // Record what AllocateNode this StoreStore protects so that
4558     // escape analysis can go from the MemBarStoreStoreNode to the
4559     // AllocateNode and eliminate the MemBarStoreStoreNode if possible
4560     // based on the escape status of the AllocateNode.
4561     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarStoreStore, alloc->proj_out_or_null(AllocateNode::RawAddress));
4562   } else {
4563     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4564   }
4565 }
4566 
4567 //------------------------inline_native_clone----------------------------
4568 // protected native Object java.lang.Object.clone();
4569 //
4570 // Here are the simple edge cases:
4571 //  null receiver => normal trap
4572 //  virtual and clone was overridden => slow path to out-of-line clone
4573 //  not cloneable or finalizer => slow path to out-of-line Object.clone
4574 //
4575 // The general case has two steps, allocation and copying.
4576 // Allocation has two cases, and uses GraphKit::new_instance or new_array.
4577 //
4578 // Copying also has two cases, oop arrays and everything else.
4579 // Oop arrays use arrayof_oop_arraycopy (same as System.arraycopy).
4580 // Everything else uses the tight inline loop supplied by CopyArrayNode.
4581 //
4582 // These steps fold up nicely if and when the cloned object's klass
4583 // can be sharply typed as an object array, a type array, or an instance.
4584 //
4585 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_clone(bool is_virtual) {
4586   PhiNode* result_val;
4587 
4588   // Set the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
4589   // the bytecode that invokes Object.clone if deoptimization happens.
4590   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
4591     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
4592 
4593     Node* obj = argument(0);
4594     if (obj->is_InlineType()) {
4595       return false;
4596     }
4597 
4598     obj = null_check_receiver();
4599     if (stopped())  return true;
4600 
4601     const TypeOopPtr* obj_type = _gvn.type(obj)->is_oopptr();
4602 
4603     // If we are going to clone an instance, we need its exact type to
4604     // know the number and types of fields to convert the clone to
4605     // loads/stores. Maybe a speculative type can help us.
4606     if (!obj_type->klass_is_exact() &&
4607         obj_type->speculative_type() != NULL &&
4608         obj_type->speculative_type()->is_instance_klass() &&
4609         !obj_type->speculative_type()->is_inlinetype()) {
4610       ciInstanceKlass* spec_ik = obj_type->speculative_type()->as_instance_klass();
4611       if (spec_ik->nof_nonstatic_fields() <= ArrayCopyLoadStoreMaxElem &&
4612           !spec_ik->has_injected_fields()) {
4613         ciKlass* k = obj_type->klass();
4614         if (!k->is_instance_klass() ||
4615             k->as_instance_klass()->is_interface() ||
4616             k->as_instance_klass()->has_subklass()) {
4617           obj = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(obj, obj_type->speculative_type(), false);
4618         }
4619       }
4620     }
4621 
4622     // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4623     // Do not let writes into the original float below the clone.
4624     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4625 
4626     // paths into result_reg:
4627     enum {
4628       _slow_path = 1,     // out-of-line call to clone method (virtual or not)
4629       _objArray_path,     // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_oop_arraycopy
4630       _array_path,        // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4631       _instance_path,     // plain instance allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4632       PATH_LIMIT
4633     };
4634     RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4635     result_val             = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL);
4636     PhiNode*    result_i_o = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4637     PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4638     record_for_igvn(result_reg);
4639 
4640     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4641     // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.
4642     // The paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4643     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4644     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4645 
4646     Node* array_ctl = generate_array_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4647     if (array_ctl != NULL) {
4648       // It's an array.
4649       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4650       set_control(array_ctl);
4651 
4652       BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4653       if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) &&
4654           (!obj_type->isa_aryptr() || !obj_type->is_aryptr()->is_not_flat())) {
4655         // Flattened inline type array may have object field that would require a
4656         // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
4657         generate_flatArray_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4658       }
4659 
4660       if (!stopped()) {
4661         Node* obj_length = load_array_length(obj);
4662         Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4663         Node* alloc_obj = new_array(obj_klass, obj_length, 0, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4664 
4665         BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4666         if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing)) {
4667           // If it is an oop array, it requires very special treatment,
4668           // because gc barriers are required when accessing the array.
4669           Node* is_obja = generate_objArray_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4670           if (is_obja != NULL) {
4671             PreserveJVMState pjvms2(this);
4672             set_control(is_obja);
4673             // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4674             Node* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(alloc_obj, NULL);
4675             ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, obj, intcon(0), alloc_obj, intcon(0), obj_length, alloc != NULL, false);
4676             ac->set_clone_oop_array();
4677             Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4678             assert(n == ac, "cannot disappear");
4679             ac->connect_outputs(this, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4680 
4681             result_reg->init_req(_objArray_path, control());
4682             result_val->init_req(_objArray_path, alloc_obj);
4683             result_i_o ->set_req(_objArray_path, i_o());
4684             result_mem ->set_req(_objArray_path, reset_memory());
4685           }
4686         }
4687         // Otherwise, there are no barriers to worry about.
4688         // (We can dispense with card marks if we know the allocation
4689         //  comes out of eden (TLAB)...  In fact, ReduceInitialCardMarks
4690         //  causes the non-eden paths to take compensating steps to
4691         //  simulate a fresh allocation, so that no further
4692         //  card marks are required in compiled code to initialize
4693         //  the object.)
4694 
4695         if (!stopped()) {
4696           copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, true);
4697 
4698           // Present the results of the copy.
4699           result_reg->init_req(_array_path, control());
4700           result_val->init_req(_array_path, alloc_obj);
4701           result_i_o ->set_req(_array_path, i_o());
4702           result_mem ->set_req(_array_path, reset_memory());
4703         }
4704       }
4705     }
4706 
4707     if (!stopped()) {
4708       // It's an instance (we did array above).  Make the slow-path tests.
4709       // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We grab
4710       // the vtable entry corresponding to clone() from the target object.
4711       // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the
4712       // Object clone() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4713       // guard for non-virtual calls; the caller is known to be the native
4714       // Object clone().
4715       if (is_virtual) {
4716         generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4717       }
4718 
4719       // The object must be easily cloneable and must not have a finalizer.
4720       // Both of these conditions may be checked in a single test.
4721       // We could optimize the test further, but we don't care.
4722       generate_access_flags_guard(obj_klass,
4723                                   // Test both conditions:
4724                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST | JVM_ACC_HAS_FINALIZER,
4725                                   // Must be cloneable but not finalizer:
4726                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST,
4727                                   slow_region);
4728     }
4729 
4730     if (!stopped()) {
4731       // It's an instance, and it passed the slow-path tests.
4732       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4733       Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4734       // Need to deoptimize on exception from allocation since Object.clone intrinsic
4735       // is reexecuted if deoptimization occurs and there could be problems when merging
4736       // exception state between multiple Object.clone versions (reexecute=true vs reexecute=false).
4737       Node* alloc_obj = new_instance(obj_klass, NULL, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4738 
4739       copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, false);
4740 
4741       // Present the results of the slow call.
4742       result_reg->init_req(_instance_path, control());
4743       result_val->init_req(_instance_path, alloc_obj);
4744       result_i_o ->set_req(_instance_path, i_o());
4745       result_mem ->set_req(_instance_path, reset_memory());
4746     }
4747 
4748     // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to clone().
4749     set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4750     if (!stopped()) {
4751       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4752       CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::_clone, is_virtual);
4753       // We need to deoptimize on exception (see comment above)
4754       Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call, false, /* deoptimize */ true);
4755       // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4756       result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4757       result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4758       result_i_o ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4759       result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4760     }
4761 
4762     // Return the combined state.
4763     set_control(    _gvn.transform(result_reg));
4764     set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_i_o));
4765     set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4766   } // original reexecute is set back here
4767 
4768   set_result(_gvn.transform(result_val));
4769   return true;
4770 }
4771 
4772 // If we have a tightly coupled allocation, the arraycopy may take care
4773 // of the array initialization. If one of the guards we insert between
4774 // the allocation and the arraycopy causes a deoptimization, an
4775 // unitialized array will escape the compiled method. To prevent that
4776 // we set the JVM state for uncommon traps between the allocation and
4777 // the arraycopy to the state before the allocation so, in case of
4778 // deoptimization, we'll reexecute the allocation and the
4779 // initialization.
4780 JVMState* LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, int& saved_reexecute_sp) {
4781   if (alloc != NULL) {
4782     ciMethod* trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
4783     int trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
4784 
4785     if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
4786         !C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_null_check)) {
4787       // Make sure there's no store between the allocation and the
4788       // arraycopy otherwise visible side effects could be rexecuted
4789       // in case of deoptimization and cause incorrect execution.
4790       bool no_interfering_store = true;
4791       Node* mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4792       if (mem->is_MergeMem()) {
4793         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory(), mem->as_MergeMem()); mms.next_non_empty2(); ) {
4794           Node* n = mms.memory();
4795           if (n != mms.memory2() && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4796             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4797             no_interfering_store = false;
4798             break;
4799           }
4800         }
4801       } else {
4802         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory()); mms.next_non_empty(); ) {
4803           Node* n = mms.memory();
4804           if (n != mem && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4805             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4806             no_interfering_store = false;
4807             break;
4808           }
4809         }
4810       }
4811 
4812       if (no_interfering_store) {
4813         JVMState* old_jvms = alloc->jvms()->clone_shallow(C);
4814         uint size = alloc->req();
4815         SafePointNode* sfpt = new SafePointNode(size, old_jvms);
4816         old_jvms->set_map(sfpt);
4817         for (uint i = 0; i < size; i++) {
4818           sfpt->init_req(i, alloc->in(i));
4819         }
4820         // re-push array length for deoptimization
4821         sfpt->ins_req(old_jvms->stkoff() + old_jvms->sp(), alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4822         old_jvms->set_sp(old_jvms->sp()+1);
4823         old_jvms->set_monoff(old_jvms->monoff()+1);
4824         old_jvms->set_scloff(old_jvms->scloff()+1);
4825         old_jvms->set_endoff(old_jvms->endoff()+1);
4826         old_jvms->set_should_reexecute(true);
4827 
4828         sfpt->set_i_o(map()->i_o());
4829         sfpt->set_memory(map()->memory());
4830         sfpt->set_control(map()->control());
4831 
4832         JVMState* saved_jvms = jvms();
4833         saved_reexecute_sp = _reexecute_sp;
4834 
4835         set_jvms(sfpt->jvms());
4836         _reexecute_sp = jvms()->sp();
4837 
4838         return saved_jvms;
4839       }
4840     }
4841   }
4842   return NULL;
4843 }
4844 
4845 // In case of a deoptimization, we restart execution at the
4846 // allocation, allocating a new array. We would leave an uninitialized
4847 // array in the heap that GCs wouldn't expect. Move the allocation
4848 // after the traps so we don't allocate the array if we
4849 // deoptimize. This is possible because tightly_coupled_allocation()
4850 // guarantees there's no observer of the allocated array at this point
4851 // and the control flow is simple enough.
4852 void LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_move_allocation_here(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, Node* dest, JVMState* saved_jvms,
4853                                                     int saved_reexecute_sp, uint new_idx) {
4854   if (saved_jvms != NULL && !stopped()) {
4855     assert(alloc != NULL, "only with a tightly coupled allocation");
4856     // restore JVM state to the state at the arraycopy
4857     saved_jvms->map()->set_control(map()->control());
4858     assert(saved_jvms->map()->memory() == map()->memory(), "memory state changed?");
4859     assert(saved_jvms->map()->i_o() == map()->i_o(), "IO state changed?");
4860     // If we've improved the types of some nodes (null check) while
4861     // emitting the guards, propagate them to the current state
4862     map()->replaced_nodes().apply(saved_jvms->map(), new_idx);
4863     set_jvms(saved_jvms);
4864     _reexecute_sp = saved_reexecute_sp;
4865 
4866     // Remove the allocation from above the guards
4867     CallProjections* callprojs = alloc->extract_projections(true);
4868     InitializeNode* init = alloc->initialization();
4869     Node* alloc_mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4870     C->gvn_replace_by(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj, alloc->in(TypeFunc::I_O));
4871     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Memory), alloc_mem);
4872     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Control), alloc->in(0));
4873 
4874     // move the allocation here (after the guards)
4875     _gvn.hash_delete(alloc);
4876     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Control, control());
4877     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::I_O, i_o());
4878     Node *mem = reset_memory();
4879     set_all_memory(mem);
4880     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Memory, mem);
4881     set_control(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Control));
4882     set_i_o(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj);
4883 
4884     // Update memory as done in GraphKit::set_output_for_allocation()
4885     const TypeInt* length_type = _gvn.find_int_type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4886     const TypeOopPtr* ary_type = _gvn.type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::KlassNode))->is_klassptr()->as_instance_type();
4887     if (ary_type->isa_aryptr() && length_type != NULL) {
4888       ary_type = ary_type->is_aryptr()->cast_to_size(length_type);
4889     }
4890     const TypePtr* telemref = ary_type->add_offset(Type::OffsetBot);
4891     int            elemidx  = C->get_alias_index(telemref);
4892     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4893     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), elemidx);
4894 
4895     Node* allocx = _gvn.transform(alloc);
4896     assert(allocx == alloc, "where has the allocation gone?");
4897     assert(dest->is_CheckCastPP(), "not an allocation result?");
4898 
4899     _gvn.hash_delete(dest);
4900     dest->set_req(0, control());
4901     Node* destx = _gvn.transform(dest);
4902     assert(destx == dest, "where has the allocation result gone?");
4903   }
4904 }
4905 
4906 
4907 //------------------------------inline_arraycopy-----------------------
4908 // public static native void java.lang.System.arraycopy(Object src,  int  srcPos,
4909 //                                                      Object dest, int destPos,
4910 //                                                      int length);
4911 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_arraycopy() {
4912   // Get the arguments.
4913   Node* src         = argument(0);  // type: oop
4914   Node* src_offset  = argument(1);  // type: int
4915   Node* dest        = argument(2);  // type: oop
4916   Node* dest_offset = argument(3);  // type: int
4917   Node* length      = argument(4);  // type: int
4918 
4919   uint new_idx = C->unique();
4920 
4921   // Check for allocation before we add nodes that would confuse
4922   // tightly_coupled_allocation()
4923   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4924 
4925   int saved_reexecute_sp = -1;
4926   JVMState* saved_jvms = arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(alloc, saved_reexecute_sp);
4927   // See arraycopy_restore_alloc_state() comment
4928   // if alloc == NULL we don't have to worry about a tightly coupled allocation so we can emit all needed guards
4929   // if saved_jvms != NULL (then alloc != NULL) then we can handle guards and a tightly coupled allocation
4930   // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we can't emit any guards
4931   bool can_emit_guards = (alloc == NULL || saved_jvms != NULL);
4932 
4933   // The following tests must be performed
4934   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4935   // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4936   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4937   // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4938   // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4939   // (6) length must not be negative.
4940   // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4941   // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4942   // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4943 
4944   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4945   // always do this here because we need the JVM state for uncommon traps
4946   Node* null_ctl = top();
4947   src  = saved_jvms != NULL ? null_check_oop(src, &null_ctl, true, true) : null_check(src,  T_ARRAY);
4948   assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
4949   dest = null_check(dest, T_ARRAY);
4950 
4951   if (!can_emit_guards) {
4952     // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we don't emit any
4953     // guards but the arraycopy node could still take advantage of a
4954     // tightly allocated allocation. tightly_coupled_allocation() is
4955     // called again to make sure it takes the null check above into
4956     // account: the null check is mandatory and if it caused an
4957     // uncommon trap to be emitted then the allocation can't be
4958     // considered tightly coupled in this context.
4959     alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4960   }
4961 
4962   bool validated = false;
4963 
4964   const Type* src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
4965   const Type* dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
4966   const TypeAryPtr* top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
4967   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
4968 
4969   // Do we have the type of src?
4970   bool has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
4971   // Do we have the type of dest?
4972   bool has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
4973   // Is the type for src from speculation?
4974   bool src_spec = false;
4975   // Is the type for dest from speculation?
4976   bool dest_spec = false;
4977 
4978   if ((!has_src || !has_dest) && can_emit_guards) {
4979     // We don't have sufficient type information, let's see if
4980     // speculative types can help. We need to have types for both src
4981     // and dest so that it pays off.
4982 
4983     // Do we already have or could we have type information for src
4984     bool could_have_src = has_src;
4985     // Do we already have or could we have type information for dest
4986     bool could_have_dest = has_dest;
4987 
4988     ciKlass* src_k = NULL;
4989     if (!has_src) {
4990       src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4991       if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
4992         could_have_src = true;
4993       }
4994     }
4995 
4996     ciKlass* dest_k = NULL;
4997     if (!has_dest) {
4998       dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
4999       if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5000         could_have_dest = true;
5001       }
5002     }
5003 
5004     if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5005       // This is going to pay off so emit the required guards
5006       if (!has_src) {
5007         src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5008         src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
5009         top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5010         has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5011         src_spec = true;
5012       }
5013       if (!has_dest) {
5014         dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5015         dest_type  = _gvn.type(dest);
5016         top_dest  = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5017         has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5018         dest_spec = true;
5019       }
5020     }
5021   }
5022 
5023   if (has_src && has_dest && can_emit_guards) {
5024     BasicType src_elem  = top_src->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5025     BasicType dest_elem = top_dest->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5026     if (is_reference_type(src_elem))   src_elem  = T_OBJECT;
5027     if (is_reference_type(dest_elem))  dest_elem = T_OBJECT;
5028 
5029     if (src_elem == dest_elem && src_elem == T_OBJECT) {
5030       // If both arrays are object arrays then having the exact types
5031       // for both will remove the need for a subtype check at runtime
5032       // before the call and may make it possible to pick a faster copy
5033       // routine (without a subtype check on every element)
5034       // Do we have the exact type of src?
5035       bool could_have_src = src_spec;
5036       // Do we have the exact type of dest?
5037       bool could_have_dest = dest_spec;
5038       ciKlass* src_k = top_src->klass();
5039       ciKlass* dest_k = top_dest->klass();
5040       if (!src_spec) {
5041         src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5042         if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5043           could_have_src = true;
5044         }
5045       }
5046       if (!dest_spec) {
5047         dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5048         if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5049           could_have_dest = true;
5050         }
5051       }
5052       if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5053         // If we can have both exact types, emit the missing guards
5054         if (could_have_src && !src_spec) {
5055           src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5056           src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5057           top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5058         }
5059         if (could_have_dest && !dest_spec) {
5060           dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5061           dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
5062           top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5063         }
5064       }
5065     }
5066   }
5067 
5068   ciMethod* trap_method = method();
5069   int trap_bci = bci();
5070   if (saved_jvms != NULL) {
5071     trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
5072     trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
5073   }
5074 
5075   bool negative_length_guard_generated = false;
5076 
5077   if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
5078       can_emit_guards &&
5079       !src->is_top() && !dest->is_top()) {
5080     // validate arguments: enables transformation the ArrayCopyNode
5081     validated = true;
5082 
5083     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
5084     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
5085 
5086     // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5087     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(src), slow_region);
5088     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(dest), slow_region);
5089 
5090     // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
5091     // done at macro expansion or at Ideal transformation time
5092 
5093     // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
5094     generate_negative_guard(src_offset, slow_region);
5095 
5096     // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
5097     generate_negative_guard(dest_offset, slow_region);
5098 
5099     // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
5100     generate_limit_guard(src_offset, length,
5101                          load_array_length(src),
5102                          slow_region);
5103 
5104     // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
5105     generate_limit_guard(dest_offset, length,
5106                          load_array_length(dest),
5107                          slow_region);
5108 
5109     // (6) length must not be negative.
5110     // This is also checked in generate_arraycopy() during macro expansion, but
5111     // we also have to check it here for the case where the ArrayCopyNode will
5112     // be eliminated by Escape Analysis.
5113     if (EliminateAllocations) {
5114       generate_negative_guard(length, slow_region);
5115       negative_length_guard_generated = true;
5116     }
5117 
5118     // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
5119     Node* dest_klass = load_object_klass(dest);
5120     if (src != dest) {
5121       Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(src, dest_klass);
5122 
5123       if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
5124         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5125         set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
5126         uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5127                       Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5128         assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5129       }
5130     }
5131 
5132     const TypeKlassPtr* dest_klass_t = _gvn.type(dest_klass)->is_klassptr();
5133     const Type* toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(dest_klass_t->klass());
5134     src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, toop));
5135     src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5136     top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5137 
5138     if (top_dest != NULL && !top_dest->is_flat() && !top_dest->is_not_flat()) {
5139       generate_flatArray_guard(dest_klass, slow_region);
5140       top_dest = top_dest->cast_to_not_flat();
5141       dest = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), dest, top_dest));
5142     }
5143     if (top_src != NULL && !top_src->is_flat() && !top_src->is_not_flat()) {
5144       Node* src_klass = load_object_klass(src);
5145       generate_flatArray_guard(src_klass, slow_region);
5146       top_src = top_src->cast_to_not_flat();
5147       src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, top_src));
5148     }
5149 
5150     {
5151       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5152       set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
5153       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5154                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5155       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5156     }
5157   }
5158 
5159   arraycopy_move_allocation_here(alloc, dest, saved_jvms, saved_reexecute_sp, new_idx);
5160 
5161   if (stopped()) {
5162     return true;
5163   }
5164 
5165   ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, src, src_offset, dest, dest_offset, length, alloc != NULL, negative_length_guard_generated,
5166                                           // Create LoadRange and LoadKlass nodes for use during macro expansion here
5167                                           // so the compiler has a chance to eliminate them: during macro expansion,
5168                                           // we have to set their control (CastPP nodes are eliminated).
5169                                           load_object_klass(src), load_object_klass(dest),
5170                                           load_array_length(src), load_array_length(dest));
5171 
5172   ac->set_arraycopy(validated);
5173 
5174   Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
5175   if (n == ac) {
5176     ac->connect_outputs(this);
5177   } else {
5178     assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
5179     set_all_memory(n);
5180   }
5181   clear_upper_avx();
5182 
5183 
5184   return true;
5185 }
5186 
5187 
5188 // Helper function which determines if an arraycopy immediately follows
5189 // an allocation, with no intervening tests or other escapes for the object.
5190 AllocateArrayNode*
5191 LibraryCallKit::tightly_coupled_allocation(Node* ptr,
5192                                            RegionNode* slow_region) {
5193   if (stopped())             return NULL;  // no fast path
5194   if (C->AliasLevel() == 0)  return NULL;  // no MergeMems around
5195 
5196   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(ptr, &_gvn);
5197   if (alloc == NULL)  return NULL;
5198 
5199   Node* rawmem = memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5200   // Is the allocation's memory state untouched?
5201   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0)->is_Initialize())) {
5202     // Bail out if there have been raw-memory effects since the allocation.
5203     // (Example:  There might have been a call or safepoint.)
5204     return NULL;
5205   }
5206   rawmem = rawmem->in(0)->as_Initialize()->memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5207   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0) == alloc)) {
5208     return NULL;
5209   }
5210 
5211   // There must be no unexpected observers of this allocation.
5212   for (DUIterator_Fast imax, i = ptr->fast_outs(imax); i < imax; i++) {
5213     Node* obs = ptr->fast_out(i);
5214     if (obs != this->map()) {
5215       return NULL;
5216     }
5217   }
5218 
5219   // This arraycopy must unconditionally follow the allocation of the ptr.
5220   Node* alloc_ctl = ptr->in(0);
5221   Node* ctl = control();
5222   while (ctl != alloc_ctl) {
5223     // There may be guards which feed into the slow_region.
5224     // Any other control flow means that we might not get a chance
5225     // to finish initializing the allocated object.
5226     if ((ctl->is_IfFalse() || ctl->is_IfTrue()) && ctl->in(0)->is_If()) {
5227       IfNode* iff = ctl->in(0)->as_If();
5228       Node* not_ctl = iff->proj_out_or_null(1 - ctl->as_Proj()->_con);
5229       assert(not_ctl != NULL && not_ctl != ctl, "found alternate");
5230       if (slow_region != NULL && slow_region->find_edge(not_ctl) >= 1) {
5231         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds the known slow_region.
5232         continue;
5233       }
5234       // One more try:  Various low-level checks bottom out in
5235       // uncommon traps.  If the debug-info of the trap omits
5236       // any reference to the allocation, as we've already
5237       // observed, then there can be no objection to the trap.
5238       bool found_trap = false;
5239       for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = not_ctl->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
5240         Node* obs = not_ctl->fast_out(j);
5241         if (obs->in(0) == not_ctl && obs->is_Call() &&
5242             (obs->as_Call()->entry_point() == SharedRuntime::uncommon_trap_blob()->entry_point())) {
5243           found_trap = true; break;
5244         }
5245       }
5246       if (found_trap) {
5247         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds a harmless uncommon trap.
5248         continue;
5249       }
5250     }
5251     return NULL;
5252   }
5253 
5254   // If we get this far, we have an allocation which immediately
5255   // precedes the arraycopy, and we can take over zeroing the new object.
5256   // The arraycopy will finish the initialization, and provide
5257   // a new control state to which we will anchor the destination pointer.
5258 
5259   return alloc;
5260 }
5261 
5262 //-------------inline_encodeISOArray-----------------------------------
5263 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5264 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_encodeISOArray() {
5265   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "encodeISOArray has 5 parameters");
5266   // no receiver since it is static method
5267   Node *src         = argument(0);
5268   Node *src_offset  = argument(1);
5269   Node *dst         = argument(2);
5270   Node *dst_offset  = argument(3);
5271   Node *length      = argument(4);
5272 
5273   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5274   dst = must_be_not_null(dst, true);
5275 
5276   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5277   const Type* dst_type = dst->Value(&_gvn);
5278   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5279   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dst_type->isa_aryptr();
5280   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL ||
5281       top_dest == NULL || top_dest->klass() == NULL) {
5282     // failed array check
5283     return false;
5284   }
5285 
5286   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5287   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5288   BasicType dst_elem = dst_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5289   if (!((src_elem == T_CHAR) || (src_elem== T_BYTE)) || dst_elem != T_BYTE) {
5290     return false;
5291   }
5292 
5293   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_CHAR);
5294   Node* dst_start = array_element_address(dst, dst_offset, dst_elem);
5295   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5296   // 'dst_start' points to dst array + scaled offset
5297 
5298   const TypeAryPtr* mtype = TypeAryPtr::BYTES;
5299   Node* enc = new EncodeISOArrayNode(control(), memory(mtype), src_start, dst_start, length);
5300   enc = _gvn.transform(enc);
5301   Node* res_mem = _gvn.transform(new SCMemProjNode(enc));
5302   set_memory(res_mem, mtype);
5303   set_result(enc);
5304   clear_upper_avx();
5305 
5306   return true;
5307 }
5308 
5309 //-------------inline_multiplyToLen-----------------------------------
5310 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_multiplyToLen() {
5311   assert(UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5312 
5313   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::multiplyToLen();
5314   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5315     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5316   }
5317   const char* stubName = "multiplyToLen";
5318 
5319   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "multiplyToLen has 5 parameters");
5320 
5321   // no receiver because it is a static method
5322   Node* x    = argument(0);
5323   Node* xlen = argument(1);
5324   Node* y    = argument(2);
5325   Node* ylen = argument(3);
5326   Node* z    = argument(4);
5327 
5328   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5329   y = must_be_not_null(y, true);
5330 
5331   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5332   const Type* y_type = y->Value(&_gvn);
5333   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5334   const TypeAryPtr* top_y = y_type->isa_aryptr();
5335   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5336       top_y == NULL || top_y->klass() == NULL) {
5337     // failed array check
5338     return false;
5339   }
5340 
5341   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5342   BasicType y_elem = y_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5343   if (x_elem != T_INT || y_elem != T_INT) {
5344     return false;
5345   }
5346 
5347   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
5348   // the bytecode that invokes BigInteger.multiplyToLen() if deoptimization happens
5349   // on the return from z array allocation in runtime.
5350   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
5351     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
5352 
5353     Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5354     Node* y_start = array_element_address(y, intcon(0), y_elem);
5355     // 'x_start' points to x array + scaled xlen
5356     // 'y_start' points to y array + scaled ylen
5357 
5358     // Allocate the result array
5359     Node* zlen = _gvn.transform(new AddINode(xlen, ylen));
5360     ciKlass* klass = ciTypeArrayKlass::make(T_INT);
5361     Node* klass_node = makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(klass));
5362 
5363     IdealKit ideal(this);
5364 
5365 #define __ ideal.
5366      Node* one = __ ConI(1);
5367      Node* zero = __ ConI(0);
5368      IdealVariable need_alloc(ideal), z_alloc(ideal);  __ declarations_done();
5369      __ set(need_alloc, zero);
5370      __ set(z_alloc, z);
5371      __ if_then(z, BoolTest::eq, null()); {
5372        __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5373      } __ else_(); {
5374        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5375        sync_kit(ideal);
5376        Node *cast = new CastPPNode(z, TypePtr::NOTNULL);
5377        cast->init_req(0, control());
5378        _gvn.set_type(cast, cast->bottom_type());
5379        C->record_for_igvn(cast);
5380 
5381        Node* zlen_arg = load_array_length(cast);
5382        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5383        __ sync_kit(this);
5384        __ if_then(zlen_arg, BoolTest::lt, zlen); {
5385          __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5386        } __ end_if();
5387      } __ end_if();
5388 
5389      __ if_then(__ value(need_alloc), BoolTest::ne, zero); {
5390        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5391        sync_kit(ideal);
5392        Node * narr = new_array(klass_node, zlen, 1);
5393        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5394        __ sync_kit(this);
5395        __ set(z_alloc, narr);
5396      } __ end_if();
5397 
5398      sync_kit(ideal);
5399      z = __ value(z_alloc);
5400      // Can't use TypeAryPtr::INTS which uses Bottom offset.
5401      _gvn.set_type(z, TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass));
5402      // Final sync IdealKit and GraphKit.
5403      final_sync(ideal);
5404 #undef __
5405 
5406     Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), T_INT);
5407 
5408     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5409                                    OptoRuntime::multiplyToLen_Type(),
5410                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5411                                    x_start, xlen, y_start, ylen, z_start, zlen);
5412   } // original reexecute is set back here
5413 
5414   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
5415   set_result(z);
5416   return true;
5417 }
5418 
5419 //-------------inline_squareToLen------------------------------------
5420 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_squareToLen() {
5421   assert(UseSquareToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5422 
5423   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::squareToLen();
5424   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5425     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5426   }
5427   const char* stubName = "squareToLen";
5428 
5429   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "implSquareToLen has 4 parameters");
5430 
5431   Node* x    = argument(0);
5432   Node* len  = argument(1);
5433   Node* z    = argument(2);
5434   Node* zlen = argument(3);
5435 
5436   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5437   z = must_be_not_null(z, true);
5438 
5439   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5440   const Type* z_type = z->Value(&_gvn);
5441   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5442   const TypeAryPtr* top_z = z_type->isa_aryptr();
5443   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5444       top_z  == NULL || top_z->klass()  == NULL) {
5445     // failed array check
5446     return false;
5447   }
5448 
5449   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5450   BasicType z_elem = z_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5451   if (x_elem != T_INT || z_elem != T_INT) {
5452     return false;
5453   }
5454 
5455 
5456   Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5457   Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), z_elem);
5458 
5459   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5460                                   OptoRuntime::squareToLen_Type(),
5461                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5462                                   x_start, len, z_start, zlen);
5463 
5464   set_result(z);
5465   return true;
5466 }

5468 //-------------inline_mulAdd------------------------------------------
5469 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_mulAdd() {
5470   assert(UseMulAddIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5471 
5472   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::mulAdd();
5473   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5474     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5475   }
5476   const char* stubName = "mulAdd";
5477 
5478   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "mulAdd has 5 parameters");
5479 
5480   Node* out      = argument(0);
5481   Node* in       = argument(1);
5482   Node* offset   = argument(2);
5483   Node* len      = argument(3);
5484   Node* k        = argument(4);
5485 
5486   out = must_be_not_null(out, true);
5487 
5488   const Type* out_type = out->Value(&_gvn);
5489   const Type* in_type = in->Value(&_gvn);
5490   const TypeAryPtr* top_out = out_type->isa_aryptr();
5491   const TypeAryPtr* top_in = in_type->isa_aryptr();
5492   if (top_out  == NULL || top_out->klass()  == NULL ||
5493       top_in == NULL || top_in->klass() == NULL) {
5494     // failed array check
5495     return false;
5496   }
5497 
5498   BasicType out_elem = out_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5499   BasicType in_elem = in_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5500   if (out_elem != T_INT || in_elem != T_INT) {
5501     return false;
5502   }
5503 
5504   Node* outlen = load_array_length(out);
5505   Node* new_offset = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(outlen, offset));
5506   Node* out_start = array_element_address(out, intcon(0), out_elem);
5507   Node* in_start = array_element_address(in, intcon(0), in_elem);
5508 
5509   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5510                                   OptoRuntime::mulAdd_Type(),
5511                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5512                                   out_start,in_start, new_offset, len, k);
5513   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5514   set_result(result);
5515   return true;
5516 }

5518 //-------------inline_montgomeryMultiply-----------------------------------
5519 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_montgomeryMultiply() {
5520   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::montgomeryMultiply();
5521   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5522     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5523   }
5524 
5525   assert(UseMontgomeryMultiplyIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5526   const char* stubName = "montgomery_multiply";
5527

5529 
5530   Node* a    = argument(0);
5531   Node* b    = argument(1);
5532   Node* n    = argument(2);
5533   Node* len  = argument(3);
5534   Node* inv  = argument(4);
5535   Node* m    = argument(6);
5536 
5537   const Type* a_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5538   const TypeAryPtr* top_a = a_type->isa_aryptr();
5539   const Type* b_type = b->Value(&_gvn);
5540   const TypeAryPtr* top_b = b_type->isa_aryptr();
5541   const Type* n_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5542   const TypeAryPtr* top_n = n_type->isa_aryptr();
5543   const Type* m_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5544   const TypeAryPtr* top_m = m_type->isa_aryptr();
5545   if (top_a  == NULL || top_a->klass()  == NULL ||
5546       top_b == NULL || top_b->klass()  == NULL ||
5547       top_n == NULL || top_n->klass()  == NULL ||
5548       top_m == NULL || top_m->klass()  == NULL) {
5549     // failed array check
5550     return false;
5551   }
5552 
5553   BasicType a_elem = a_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5554   BasicType b_elem = b_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5555   BasicType n_elem = n_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5556   BasicType m_elem = m_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5557   if (a_elem != T_INT || b_elem != T_INT || n_elem != T_INT || m_elem != T_INT) {
5558     return false;
5559   }
5560 
5561   // Make the call
5562   {
5563     Node* a_start = array_element_address(a, intcon(0), a_elem);
5564     Node* b_start = array_element_address(b, intcon(0), b_elem);
5565     Node* n_start = array_element_address(n, intcon(0), n_elem);
5566     Node* m_start = array_element_address(m, intcon(0), m_elem);
5567 
5568     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5569                                    OptoRuntime::montgomeryMultiply_Type(),
5570                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5571                                    a_start, b_start, n_start, len, inv, top(),
5572                                    m_start);
5573     set_result(m);
5574   }
5575 
5576   return true;
5577 }

5633 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_bigIntegerShift(bool isRightShift) {
5634   address stubAddr = NULL;
5635   const char* stubName = NULL;
5636 
5637   stubAddr = isRightShift? StubRoutines::bigIntegerRightShift(): StubRoutines::bigIntegerLeftShift();
5638   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5639     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5640   }
5641 
5642   stubName = isRightShift? "bigIntegerRightShiftWorker" : "bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker";
5643 
5644   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "expected 5 arguments");
5645 
5646   Node* newArr = argument(0);
5647   Node* oldArr = argument(1);
5648   Node* newIdx = argument(2);
5649   Node* shiftCount = argument(3);
5650   Node* numIter = argument(4);
5651 
5652   const Type* newArr_type = newArr->Value(&_gvn);
5653   const TypeAryPtr* top_newArr = newArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5654   const Type* oldArr_type = oldArr->Value(&_gvn);
5655   const TypeAryPtr* top_oldArr = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5656   if (top_newArr == NULL || top_newArr->klass() == NULL || top_oldArr == NULL
5657       || top_oldArr->klass() == NULL) {
5658     return false;
5659   }
5660 
5661   BasicType newArr_elem = newArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5662   BasicType oldArr_elem = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5663   if (newArr_elem != T_INT || oldArr_elem != T_INT) {
5664     return false;
5665   }
5666 
5667   // Make the call
5668   {
5669     Node* newArr_start = array_element_address(newArr, intcon(0), newArr_elem);
5670     Node* oldArr_start = array_element_address(oldArr, intcon(0), oldArr_elem);
5671 
5672     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5673                                    OptoRuntime::bigIntegerShift_Type(),
5674                                    stubAddr,
5675                                    stubName,
5676                                    TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5677                                    newArr_start,
5678                                    oldArr_start,
5679                                    newIdx,
5680                                    shiftCount,
5681                                    numIter);
5682   }
5683 
5684   return true;
5685 }

5690

5692   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5693     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5694   }

5696   int size_l = callee()->signature()->size();

5700   Node* aoffset = argument(1);
