5732 /**
5733  * Calculate CRC32 for byte.
5734  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.update(int crc, int b)
5735  */
5736 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateCRC32() {
5737   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5738   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "update has 2 parameters");
5739   // no receiver since it is static method
5740   Node* crc  = argument(0); // type: int
5741   Node* b    = argument(1); // type: int
5742 
5743   /*
5744    *    int c = ~ crc;
5745    *    b = timesXtoThe32[(b ^ c) & 0xFF];
5746    *    b = b ^ (c >>> 8);
5747    *    crc = ~b;
5748    */
5749 
5750   Node* M1 = intcon(-1);
5751   crc = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, M1));
5752   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, b));
5753   result = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(result, intcon(0xFF)));
5754 
5755   Node* base = makecon(TypeRawPtr::make(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
5756   Node* offset = _gvn.transform(new LShiftINode(result, intcon(0x2)));
5757   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, ConvI2X(offset));
5758   result = make_load(control(), adr, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
5759 
5760   crc = _gvn.transform(new URShiftINode(crc, intcon(8)));
5761   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, result));
5762   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(result, M1));
5763   set_result(result);
5764   return true;
5765 }
5766 
5767 /**
5768  * Calculate CRC32 for byte[] array.
5769  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5770  */
5771 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32() {
5772   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5773   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5774   // no receiver since it is static method
5775   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5776   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5777   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5778   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5779 
5780   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5781   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5782   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5783     // failed array check
5784     return false;
5785   }
5786 
5787   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5788   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5789   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5790     return false;
5791   }
5792 
5793   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5794   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5795   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5796 
5797   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5798   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5799 
5800   // Call the stub.
5801   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5802   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5803 
5804   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5805                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5806                                  crc, src_start, length);
5807   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5808   set_result(result);
5809   return true;
5810 }

5812 /**
5813  * Calculate CRC32 for ByteBuffer.
5814  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5815  */
5816 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferCRC32() {
5817   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5818   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5819   // no receiver since it is static method
5820   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5821   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5822   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5823   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
5824 
5825   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5826   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5827   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5828 
5829   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5830   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5831 
5832   // Call the stub.
5833   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5834   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5835 
5836   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5837                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5838                                  crc, src_start, length);
5839   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5840   set_result(result);
5841   return true;
5842 }

5844 //------------------------------get_table_from_crc32c_class-----------------------
5845 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_table_from_crc32c_class(ciInstanceKlass *crc32c_class) {
5846   Node* table = load_field_from_object(NULL, "byteTable", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false, /*is_static*/ true, crc32c_class);
5847   assert (table != NULL, "wrong version of java.util.zip.CRC32C");
5848 
5849   return table;
5850 }

5856 //
5857 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32C() {

5860   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "CRC32C class must be loaded");
5861   // no receiver since it is a static method
5862   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5863   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5864   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5865   Node* end     = argument(3); // type: int
5866

5868

5870   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();

5872     // failed array check
5873     return false;

5877   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();

5899                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,

5952 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesAdler32() {
5953   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
5954   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5955   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
5956   // no receiver since it is static method
5957   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int

5960   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int

5964   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5965     // failed array check

5967   }
5968 
5969   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5970   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5971   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5972     return false;
5973   }
5974 
5975   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5976   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5977 
5978   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5979   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5980 
5981   // Call the stub.
5982   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
5983   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
5984 
5985   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
5986                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5987                                  crc, src_start, length);
5988   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5989   set_result(result);
5990   return true;
5991 }
5992 
5993 //------------------------------inline_updateByteBufferAdler32---------------
5994 //
5995 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for DirectByteBuffer.
5996 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5997 //
5998 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferAdler32() {
5999   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
6000   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
6001   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
6002   // no receiver since it is static method
6003   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
6004   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
6005   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
6006   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
6007 
6008   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
6009   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
6010   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
6011 
6012   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6013   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
6014 
6015   // Call the stub.
6016   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6017   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6018 
6019   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6020                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6021                                  crc, src_start, length);
6022 
6023   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6024   set_result(result);
6025   return true;
6026 }
6027 
6028 //----------------------------inline_reference_get----------------------------
6029 // public T java.lang.ref.Reference.get();
6030 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_reference_get() {
6031   const int referent_offset = java_lang_ref_Reference::referent_offset();
6032 
6033   // Get the argument:
6034   Node* reference_obj = null_check_receiver();
6035   if (stopped()) return true;
6036 
6037   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(reference_obj)->isa_instptr();
6038   assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6039   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6040   ciInstanceKlass* referenceKlass = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6041   ciField* field = referenceKlass->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make("referent"),
6042                                                      ciSymbol::make("Ljava/lang/Object;"),
6043                                                      false);
6044   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6045 
6046   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(reference_obj, reference_obj, referent_offset);
6047   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6048 
6049   ciInstanceKlass* klass = env()->Object_klass();
6050   const TypeOopPtr* object_type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass);
6051 
6052   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP | ON_WEAK_OOP_REF;
6053   Node* result = access_load_at(reference_obj, adr, adr_type, object_type, T_OBJECT, decorators);
6054   // Add memory barrier to prevent commoning reads from this field
6055   // across safepoint since GC can change its value.
6056   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
6057 
6058   set_result(result);
6059   return true;
6060 }
6061 
6062 
6063 Node * LibraryCallKit::load_field_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6064                                               bool is_exact=true, bool is_static=false,
6065                                               ciInstanceKlass * fromKls=NULL) {
6066   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6067     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6068     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6069     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6070     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6071     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6072   } else {
6073     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6074   }
6075   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6076                                               ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6077                                               is_static);
6078 
6079   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6080   if (field == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6081 
6082   if (is_static) {
6083     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6084     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6085   }
6086 
6087   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6088 
6089   // Compute address and memory type.
6090   int offset  = field->offset_in_bytes();
6091   bool is_vol = field->is_volatile();
6092   ciType* field_klass = field->type();
6093   assert(field_klass->is_loaded(), "should be loaded");
6094   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6095   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6096   BasicType bt = field->layout_type();
6097 
6098   // Build the resultant type of the load
6099   const Type *type;
6100   if (bt == T_OBJECT) {
6101     type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(field_klass->as_klass());
6102   } else {
6103     type = Type::get_const_basic_type(bt);
6104   }
6105 
6106   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP;
6107 
6108   if (is_vol) {
6109     decorators |= MO_SEQ_CST;
6110   }
6111 
6112   return access_load_at(fromObj, adr, adr_type, type, bt, decorators);
6113 }
6114 
6115 Node * LibraryCallKit::field_address_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6116                                                  bool is_exact = true, bool is_static = false,
6117                                                  ciInstanceKlass * fromKls = NULL) {
6118   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6119     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6120     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6121     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6122     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6123     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6124   }
6125   else {
6126     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6127   }
6128   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6129     ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6130     is_static);
6131 
6132   assert(field != NULL, "undefined field");
6133   assert(!field->is_volatile(), "not defined for volatile fields");
6134 
6135   if (is_static) {
6136     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6137     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6138   }
6139 
6140   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6141 
6142   // Compute address and memory type.
6143   int offset = field->offset_in_bytes();
6144   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6145 
6146   return adr;
6147 }

6149 //------------------------------inline_aescrypt_Block-----------------------
6150 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_aescrypt_Block(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6151   address stubAddr = NULL;
6152   const char *stubName;
6153   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6154 
6155   switch(id) {
6156   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_encryptBlock:
6157     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_encryptBlock();
6158     stubName = "aescrypt_encryptBlock";
6159     break;
6160   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_decryptBlock:
6161     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_decryptBlock();
6162     stubName = "aescrypt_decryptBlock";
6163     break;
6164   default:
6165     break;
6166   }
6167   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6168 
6169   Node* aescrypt_object = argument(0);
6170   Node* src             = argument(1);
6171   Node* src_offset      = argument(2);
6172   Node* dest            = argument(3);
6173   Node* dest_offset     = argument(4);
6174 
6175   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6176   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6177 
6178   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6179   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6180   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6181   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6182   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6183   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6184 
6185   // for the quick and dirty code we will skip all the checks.
6186   // we are just trying to get the call to be generated.
6187   Node* src_start  = src;
6188   Node* dest_start = dest;
6189   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6190     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6191     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6192     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6193   }
6194 
6195   // now need to get the start of its expanded key array
6196   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6197   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6198   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6199 
6200   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6201     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6202     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6203     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6204     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6205 
6206     // Call the stub.
6207     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6208                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6209                       src_start, dest_start, k_start, original_k_start);
6210   } else {
6211     // Call the stub.
6212     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6213                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6214                       src_start, dest_start, k_start);
6215   }
6216 
6217   return true;
6218 }
6219 
6220 //------------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt-----------------------
6221 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6222   address stubAddr = NULL;
6223   const char *stubName = NULL;
6224 
6225   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6226 
6227   switch(id) {
6228   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt:
6229     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
6230     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt";
6231     break;
6232   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt:
6233     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt();
6234     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt";
6235     break;
6236   default:
6237     break;
6238   }
6239   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6240 
6241   Node* cipherBlockChaining_object = argument(0);
6242   Node* src                        = argument(1);
6243   Node* src_offset                 = argument(2);
6244   Node* len                        = argument(3);
6245   Node* dest                       = argument(4);
6246   Node* dest_offset                = argument(5);
6247 
6248   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6249   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, false);
6250 
6251   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6252   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6253   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6254   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6255   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6256   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL
6257           &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6258 
6259   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6260   Node* src_start  = src;
6261   Node* dest_start = dest;
6262   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6263     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6264     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6265     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6266   }
6267 
6268   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6269   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6270   // so we cast it here safely.
6271   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6272 
6273   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6274   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6275 
6276   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6277   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(cipherBlockChaining_object)->isa_instptr();
6278   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBC obj is null");
6279   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBC obj is not loaded");
6280   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6281   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6282 
6283   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6284   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6285   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6286   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6287   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6288 
6289   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6290   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6291   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6292 
6293   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6294   Node* objRvec = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "r", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6295   if (objRvec == NULL) return false;
6296   Node* r_start = array_element_address(objRvec, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6297 
6298   Node* cbcCrypt;
6299   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6300     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6301     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6302     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6303     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6304 
6305     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, src_len and original_k_start
6306     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6307                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6308                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6309                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len, original_k_start);
6310   } else {
6311     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6312     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6313                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6314                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6315                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len);
6316   }
6317 
6318   // return cipher length (int)
6319   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(cbcCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6320   set_result(retvalue);
6321   return true;
6322 }

6461   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6462   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6463   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6464   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6465   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6466   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6467   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6468   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6469   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6470   Node* obj_counter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "counter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6471   if (obj_counter == NULL) return false;
6472   Node* cnt_start = array_element_address(obj_counter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6473 
6474   Node* saved_encCounter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "encryptedCounter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6475   if (saved_encCounter == NULL) return false;
6476   Node* saved_encCounter_start = array_element_address(saved_encCounter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6477   Node* used = field_address_from_object(counterMode_object, "used", "I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6478 
6479   Node* ctrCrypt;
6480   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6481     // no SPARC version for AES/CTR intrinsics now.
6482     return false;
6483   }
6484   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6485   ctrCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6486                                OptoRuntime::counterMode_aescrypt_Type(),
6487                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6488                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, cnt_start, len, saved_encCounter_start, used);
6489 
6490   // return cipher length (int)
6491   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ctrCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6492   set_result(retvalue);
6493   return true;
6494 }
6495 
6496 //------------------------------get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6497 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6498 #if defined(PPC64) || defined(S390)
6499   // MixColumns for decryption can be reduced by preprocessing MixColumns with round keys.
6500   // Intel's extention is based on this optimization and AESCrypt generates round keys by preprocessing MixColumns.
6501   // However, ppc64 vncipher processes MixColumns and requires the same round keys with encryption.
6502   // The ppc64 stubs of encryption and decryption use the same round keys (sessionK[0]).
6503   Node* objSessionK = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "sessionK", "[[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6504   assert (objSessionK != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6505   if (objSessionK == NULL) {
6506     return (Node *) NULL;
6507   }
6508   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_array_element(control(), objSessionK, intcon(0), TypeAryPtr::OOPS);
6509 #else
6510   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "K", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6511 #endif // PPC64
6512   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6513   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6514 
6515   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the K array
6516   Node* k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_INT);
6517   return k_start;
6518 }
6519 
6520 //------------------------------get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6521 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6522   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "lastKey", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6523   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6524   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6525 
6526   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the lastKey array
6527   Node* original_k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6528   return original_k_start;
6529 }
6530 
6531 //----------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6532 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6533 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6534 // for encryption:
6535 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6536 // for decryption:
6537 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6538 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6539 //
6540 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6541   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6542   Node* objCBC = argument(0);
6543 
6544   Node* src = argument(1);
6545   Node* dest = argument(4);
6546 
6547   // Load embeddedCipher field of CipherBlockChaining object.
6548   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objCBC, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6549 
6550   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6551   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6552   // will have same classloader as CipherBlockChaining object
6553   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objCBC)->isa_instptr();
6554   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBCobj is null");
6555   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBCobj is not loaded");
6556 
6557   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6558   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6559   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6560     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6561     Node* ctrl = control();
6562     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6563     return ctrl;
6564   }
6565 
6566   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6567   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6568 
6569   // Resolve oops to stable for CmpP below.
6570   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6571 
6572   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6573   Node* cmp_instof  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6574   Node* bool_instof  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6575 
6576   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6577 
6578   // for encryption, we are done
6579   if (!decrypting)
6580     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6581 
6582   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6583   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6584   // see the original java code for why.
6585   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6586   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6587 
6588   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6589   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6590   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6591   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6592 
6593   record_for_igvn(region);
6594   return _gvn.transform(region);
6595 }
6596 
6597 //----------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6598 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6599 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6600 // for encryption:
6601 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6602 // for decryption:
6603 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6604 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6605 //
6606 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6607   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6608   Node* objECB = argument(0);
6609 
6610   // Load embeddedCipher field of ElectronicCodeBook object.
6611   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objECB, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6612 
6613   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6614   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6615   // will have same classloader as ElectronicCodeBook object
6616   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objECB)->isa_instptr();
6617   assert(tinst != NULL, "ECBobj is null");
6618   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "ECBobj is not loaded");
6619 
6620   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6621   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6622   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6623     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6624     Node* ctrl = control();
6625     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6626     return ctrl;
6627   }
6628   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6629 
6630   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6631   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6632   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6633 
6634   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6635 
6636   // for encryption, we are done
6637   if (!decrypting)
6638     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6639 
6640   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6641   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6642   // see the original java code for why.
6643   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6644   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6645   Node* src = argument(1);
6646   Node* dest = argument(4);
6647   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6648   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6649   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6650   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6651 
6652   record_for_igvn(region);
6653   return _gvn.transform(region);
6654 }

6698 //------------------------------inline_ghash_processBlocks
6699 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_ghash_processBlocks() {
6700   address stubAddr;
6701   const char *stubName;
6702   assert(UseGHASHIntrinsics, "need GHASH intrinsics support");
6703 
6704   stubAddr = StubRoutines::ghash_processBlocks();
6705   stubName = "ghash_processBlocks";
6706 
6707   Node* data           = argument(0);
6708   Node* offset         = argument(1);
6709   Node* len            = argument(2);
6710   Node* state          = argument(3);
6711   Node* subkeyH        = argument(4);
6712 
6713   state = must_be_not_null(state, true);
6714   subkeyH = must_be_not_null(subkeyH, true);
6715   data = must_be_not_null(data, true);
6716 
6717   Node* state_start  = array_element_address(state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6718   assert(state_start, "state is NULL");
6719   Node* subkeyH_start  = array_element_address(subkeyH, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6720   assert(subkeyH_start, "subkeyH is NULL");
6721   Node* data_start  = array_element_address(data, offset, T_BYTE);
6722   assert(data_start, "data is NULL");
6723 
6724   Node* ghash = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6725                                   OptoRuntime::ghash_processBlocks_Type(),
6726                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6727                                   state_start, subkeyH_start, data_start, len);
6728   return true;
6729 }

6763 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompress-----------------------
6764 //
6765 // Calculate SHA (i.e., SHA-1) for single-block byte[] array.
6766 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6767 //
6768 // Calculate SHA2 (i.e., SHA-244 or SHA-256) for single-block byte[] array.
6769 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA2.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6770 //
6771 // Calculate SHA5 (i.e., SHA-384 or SHA-512) for single-block byte[] array.
6772 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA5.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6773 //
6774 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompress(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6775   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "sha_implCompress has 2 parameters");
6776 
6777   Node* sha_obj = argument(0);
6778   Node* src     = argument(1); // type oop
6779   Node* ofs     = argument(2); // type int
6780 
6781   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6782   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6783   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6784     // failed array check
6785     return false;
6786   }
6787   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6788   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6789   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6790     return false;
6791   }
6792   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6793   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6794   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6795   Node* state = NULL;
6796   address stubAddr;
6797   const char *stubName;
6798 
6799   switch(id) {
6800   case vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress:
6801     assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics, "need SHA1 instruction support");
6802     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6803     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompress();
6804     stubName = "sha1_implCompress";
6805     break;
6806   case vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress:
6807     assert(UseSHA256Intrinsics, "need SHA256 instruction support");
6808     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6809     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompress();
6810     stubName = "sha256_implCompress";
6811     break;
6812   case vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress:
6813     assert(UseSHA512Intrinsics, "need SHA512 instruction support");
6814     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6815     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompress();
6816     stubName = "sha512_implCompress";
6817     break;
6818   default:
6819     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6820     return false;
6821   }
6822   if (state == NULL) return false;
6823 
6824   assert(stubAddr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6825   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6826 
6827   // Call the stub.
6828   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::sha_implCompress_Type(),
6829                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6830                                  src_start, state);
6831 
6832   return true;
6833 }
6834 
6835 //------------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB-----------------------
6836 //
6837 // Calculate SHA/SHA2/SHA5 for multi-block byte[] array.
6838 // int com.sun.security.provider.DigestBase.implCompressMultiBlock(byte[] b, int ofs, int limit)
6839 //
6840 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB(int predicate) {
6841   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6842          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6843   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6844   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "digestBase_implCompressMB has 3 parameters");
6845 
6846   Node* digestBase_obj = argument(0); // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6847   Node* src            = argument(1); // byte[] array
6848   Node* ofs            = argument(2); // type int
6849   Node* limit          = argument(3); // type int
6850 
6851   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6852   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6853   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6854     // failed array check
6855     return false;
6856   }
6857   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6858   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6859   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6860     return false;
6861   }
6862   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6863   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6864   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6865 
6866   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6867   const char* stub_name = NULL;
6868   address     stub_addr = NULL;
6869   bool        long_state = false;
6870 
6871   switch (predicate) {
6872   case 0:
6873     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress)) {
6874       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6875       stub_name = "sha1_implCompressMB";
6876       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompressMB();
6877     }
6878     break;
6879   case 1:
6880     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress)) {
6881       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6882       stub_name = "sha256_implCompressMB";
6883       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompressMB();
6884     }
6885     break;
6886   case 2:
6887     if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress)) {
6888       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6889       stub_name = "sha512_implCompressMB";
6890       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompressMB();
6891       long_state = true;
6892     }
6893     break;
6894   default:
6895     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6896   }
6897   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6898     assert(stub_addr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6899     if (stub_addr == NULL) return false;
6900 
6901     // get DigestBase klass to lookup for SHA klass
6902     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBase_obj)->isa_instptr();
6903     assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBase_obj is not instance???");
6904     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6905 
6906     ciKlass* klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6907     assert(klass_SHA->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6908     ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6909     return inline_sha_implCompressMB(digestBase_obj, instklass_SHA, long_state, stub_addr, stub_name, src_start, ofs, limit);
6910   }
6911   return false;
6912 }
6913 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompressMB-----------------------
6914 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompressMB(Node* digestBase_obj, ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA,
6915                                                bool long_state, address stubAddr, const char *stubName,
6916                                                Node* src_start, Node* ofs, Node* limit) {
6917   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA);
6918   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6919   Node* sha_obj = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), digestBase_obj, xtype);
6920   sha_obj = _gvn.transform(sha_obj);
6921 
6922   Node* state;
6923   if (long_state) {
6924     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6925   } else {
6926     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6927   }
6928   if (state == NULL) return false;
6929 
6930   // Call the stub.
6931   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6932                                  OptoRuntime::digestBase_implCompressMB_Type(),
6933                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6934                                  src_start, state, ofs, limit);
6935   // return ofs (int)
6936   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6937   set_result(result);
6938 
6939   return true;
6940 }
6941 
6942 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha_object-----------------------
6943 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha_object(Node *sha_object) {
6944   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6945   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA/SHA2");
6946   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6947 
6948   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6949   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_INT);
6950   return state;
6951 }
6952 
6953 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha5_object-----------------------
6954 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha5_object(Node *sha_object) {
6955   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[J", /*is_exact*/ false);
6956   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA5");
6957   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6958 
6959   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6960   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6961   return state;
6962 }
6963 
6964 //----------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate----------------------------
6965 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6966 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6967 //    if (digestBaseObj instanceof SHA/SHA2/SHA5) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6968 //
6969 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate(int predicate) {
6970   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6971          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6972   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6973 
6974   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6975   Node* digestBaseObj = argument(0);
6976 
6977   // get DigestBase klass for instanceOf check
6978   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBaseObj)->isa_instptr();
6979   assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBaseObj is null");
6980   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6981 
6982   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6983   switch (predicate) {
6984   case 0:
6985     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6986       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA class
6987       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6988     }
6989     break;
6990   case 1:
6991     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6992       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA2 class
6993       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6994     }
6995     break;
6996   case 2:
6997     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6998       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA5 class
6999       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
7000     }
7001     break;
7002   default:
7003     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
7004   }
7005 
7006   ciKlass* klass_SHA = NULL;
7007   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
7008     klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
7009   }
7010   if ((klass_SHA == NULL) || !klass_SHA->is_loaded()) {
7011     // if none of SHA/SHA2/SHA5 is loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
7012     Node* ctrl = control();
7013     set_control(top()); // no intrinsic path
7014     return ctrl;
7015   }
7016   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
7017 
7018   Node* instofSHA = gen_instanceof(digestBaseObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA)));
7019   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instofSHA, intcon(1)));
7020   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
7021   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
7022 
7023   return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
7024 }
7025 
7026 //-------------inline_fma-----------------------------------
7027 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fma(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7028   Node *a = NULL;
7029   Node *b = NULL;
7030   Node *c = NULL;
7031   Node* result = NULL;
7032   switch (id) {
7033   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaD:
7034     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 6, "fma has 3 parameters of size 2 each.");
7035     // no receiver since it is static method
7036     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7037     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7038     c = round_double_node(argument(4));
7039     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaDNode(control(), a, b, c));
7040     break;
7041   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaF:
7042     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "fma has 3 parameters of size 1 each.");
7043     a = argument(0);
7044     b = argument(1);
7045     c = argument(2);
7046     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaFNode(control(), a, b, c));
7047     break;
7048   default:
7049     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7050   }
7051   set_result(result);
7052   return true;
7053 }
7054 
7055 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_character_compare(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7056   // argument(0) is receiver
7057   Node* codePoint = argument(1);
7058   Node* n = NULL;
7059 
7060   switch (id) {
7061     case vmIntrinsics::_isDigit :
7062       n = new DigitNode(control(), codePoint);
7063       break;
7064     case vmIntrinsics::_isLowerCase :
7065       n = new LowerCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7066       break;
7067     case vmIntrinsics::_isUpperCase :
7068       n = new UpperCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7069       break;
7070     case vmIntrinsics::_isWhitespace :
7071       n = new WhitespaceNode(control(), codePoint);
7072       break;
7073     default:
7074       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7075   }
7076 
7077   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7078   return true;
7079 }
7080 
7081 //------------------------------inline_fp_min_max------------------------------
7082 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7083 /* DISABLED BECAUSE METHOD DATA ISN'T COLLECTED PER CALL-SITE, SEE JDK-8015416.
7084 
7085   // The intrinsic should be used only when the API branches aren't predictable,
7086   // the last one performing the most important comparison. The following heuristic
7087   // uses the branch statistics to eventually bail out if necessary.
7088 
7089   ciMethodData *md = callee()->method_data();
7090 
7091   if ( md != NULL && md->is_mature() && md->invocation_count() > 0 ) {
7092     ciCallProfile cp = caller()->call_profile_at_bci(bci());
7093 
7094     if ( ((double)cp.count()) / ((double)md->invocation_count()) < 0.8 ) {
7095       // Bail out if the call-site didn't contribute enough to the statistics.
7096       return false;
7097     }
7098 
7099     uint taken = 0, not_taken = 0;
7100 
7101     for (ciProfileData *p = md->first_data(); md->is_valid(p); p = md->next_data(p)) {
7102       if (p->is_BranchData()) {
7103         taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->taken();
7104         not_taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->not_taken();
7105       }
7106     }
7107 
7108     double balance = (((double)taken) - ((double)not_taken)) / ((double)md->invocation_count());
7109     balance = balance < 0 ? -balance : balance;
7110     if ( balance > 0.2 ) {
7111       // Bail out if the most important branch is predictable enough.
7112       return false;
7113     }
7114   }
7115 */
7116 
7117   Node *a = NULL;
7118   Node *b = NULL;
7119   Node *n = NULL;
7120   switch (id) {
7121   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:
7122   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:
7123     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "minF/maxF has 2 parameters of size 1 each.");
7124     a = argument(0);
7125     b = argument(1);
7126     break;
7127   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:
7128   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:
7129     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "minD/maxD has 2 parameters of size 2 each.");
7130     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7131     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7132     break;
7133   default:
7134     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7135     break;
7136   }
7137   switch (id) {
7138   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:  n = new MaxFNode(a, b);  break;
7139   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:  n = new MinFNode(a, b);  break;
7140   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:  n = new MaxDNode(a, b);  break;
7141   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:  n = new MinDNode(a, b);  break;
7142   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7143   }
7144   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7145   return true;
7146 }
7147 
7148 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_profileBoolean() {
7149   Node* counts = argument(1);
7150   const TypeAryPtr* ary = NULL;
7151   ciArray* aobj = NULL;
7152   if (counts->is_Con()
7153       && (ary = counts->bottom_type()->isa_aryptr()) != NULL
7154       && (aobj = ary->const_oop()->as_array()) != NULL
7155       && (aobj->length() == 2)) {
7156     // Profile is int[2] where [0] and [1] correspond to false and true value occurrences respectively.
7157     jint false_cnt = aobj->element_value(0).as_int();
7158     jint  true_cnt = aobj->element_value(1).as_int();
7159 
7160     if (C->log() != NULL) {
7161       C->log()->elem("observe source='profileBoolean' false='%d' true='%d'",
7162                      false_cnt, true_cnt);
7163     }
7164 
7165     if (false_cnt + true_cnt == 0) {
7166       // According to profile, never executed.
7167       uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7168                           Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7169       return true;
7170     }
7171 
7172     // result is a boolean (0 or 1) and its profile (false_cnt & true_cnt)
7173     // is a number of each value occurrences.
7174     Node* result = argument(0);
7175     if (false_cnt == 0 || true_cnt == 0) {
7176       // According to profile, one value has been never seen.
7177       int expected_val = (false_cnt == 0) ? 1 : 0;
7178 
7179       Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(result, intcon(expected_val)));
7180       Node* test = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::eq));
7181 
7182       IfNode* check = create_and_map_if(control(), test, PROB_ALWAYS, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
7183       Node* fast_path = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(check));
7184       Node* slow_path = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(check));
7185 
7186       { // Slow path: uncommon trap for never seen value and then reexecute
7187         // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() to bump the count, so JIT knows
7188         // the value has been seen at least once.
7189         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
7190         PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
7191         jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
7192 
7193         set_control(slow_path);
7194         set_i_o(i_o());
7195 
7196         uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7197                             Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7198       }
7199       // The guard for never seen value enables sharpening of the result and
7200       // returning a constant. It allows to eliminate branches on the same value
7201       // later on.
7202       set_control(fast_path);
7203       result = intcon(expected_val);
7204     }
7205     // Stop profiling.
7206     // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() has profiling logic in its bytecode.
7207     // By replacing method body with profile data (represented as ProfileBooleanNode
7208     // on IR level) we effectively disable profiling.
7209     // It enables full speed execution once optimized code is generated.
7210     Node* profile = _gvn.transform(new ProfileBooleanNode(result, false_cnt, true_cnt));
7211     C->record_for_igvn(profile);
7212     set_result(profile);
7213     return true;
7214   } else {
7215     // Continue profiling.
7216     // Profile data isn't available at the moment. So, execute method's bytecode version.
7217     // Usually, when GWT LambdaForms are profiled it means that a stand-alone nmethod
7218     // is compiled and counters aren't available since corresponding MethodHandle
7219     // isn't a compile-time constant.
7220     return false;
7221   }
7222 }
7223 
7224 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_isCompileConstant() {
7225   Node* n = argument(0);
7226   set_result(n->is_Con() ? intcon(1) : intcon(0));
7227   return true;
7228 }
